25:T19c9,<entryFree id="n2839" key="بَعْثٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">بَعْثٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">عث</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">بعث</orth>
                  </form> signifies The <hi rend="ital">removing of that which restrains one from free action.</hi> (TA.) [And hence,]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَهُ</foreign>, (S, A, &amp;c.,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">بَعَثَ</orth>
                  </form>, (A, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثٌ</foreign> (Mgh, L, Msb, TA) and <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثٌ</foreign>, (L, TA,) <hi rend="ital">He sent him;</hi> (S, A, Mgh, Msb, K;) namely, a messenger; (Msb;) and, when said of God, an apostle; (A;) [and when said of a man, a letter, &amp;c.;] as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2839-1" target="ابتعثه" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>: (S, A, Msb, K:) [or] the former is said of anything that goes, or is sent, by itself; and of anything that will not go, or be sent, by itself, as a letter, and a present, one says, <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ بِهِ</foreign>: (Msb:) [thus,] <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَهُ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">he sent him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, alone, by himself,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">by itself;</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ بِهِ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">he sent him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, by,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">with, another,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">others:</hi> (L:) but El-Fárábee says that the former of these two has another signification, which will be found below; and that the latter signifies <hi rend="ital">he sent him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it.</hi> (Msb.) Hence, <foreign lang="ar">ضُرِبَ عَلَيْهِمُ البَعْثُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The being sent to the war was appointed them and imposed upon them as an obligation.</hi> (Msb.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَهُ لِكَذَا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He sent him for such a thing</hi> or <hi rend="ital">purpose</hi>]. (A, TA.) [And <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ إِلَيْهِ بِكَذَا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He sent to him such a thing;</hi> lit., <hi rend="ital">he sent to him</hi> a messenger <hi rend="ital">with such a thing.</hi>] And <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ الجُنْدَ إِلَى الغَزْوِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He sent the army to the war</hi>]. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ عَلَيْهِمُ البَلَآءَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He sent upon them trial,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">affliction;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">he caused trial,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">affliction, to befall them.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Also, (A, L, TA,) inf. <foreign lang="ar">بَعْثٌ</foreign> (Mgh, L, TA) and <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثٌ</foreign> (L) and <foreign lang="ar">تَبْعَاثٌ</foreign> [an intensive form], (TA,) <hi rend="ital">He roused him, excited him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">put him in motion</hi> or <hi rend="ital">action;</hi> (A, L, Mgh, TA;) namely, anything; (TA;) [i. e. any person or animal; and particularly,] an animal lying down, or a person sitting. (L, TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ النَّاقَةَ</foreign> 
                  <pb n="223"/> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He roused,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">put in motion</hi> or <hi rend="ital">action, the she-camel;</hi> (S, Mgh, K, TA;) i. e., <hi rend="ital">loosed the cord that bound her shank to her arm, and dismissed her;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he roused her,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">made her to rise, she being lying down.</hi> (TA.) It is said in a trad. respecting 'Áïsheh, <foreign lang="ar">فَبَعَثْنَا البَعِيرَ فإِذَا العِقْدُ تَحْتَهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And we made the camel to rise, and to, the necklace was beneath him</hi>]. (TA.) You say also, <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَهُ عَلَى الأَمْرِ</foreign>, (A,) or <foreign lang="ar">الشَّىْءِ</foreign>, (L,) <hi rend="ital">He roused him, excited him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">put him in motion</hi> or <hi rend="ital">action, to do the affair,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">thing:</hi> (A:) or <hi rend="ital">he incited him, urged him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">instigated him, to do the thing.</hi> (L.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  Also, accord. to El-Fárábee, (Msb,) or <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَهُ مِنْ مَنَامِهِ</foreign>, (S, A, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثٌ</foreign>, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">He roused him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">awoke him, from his sleep;</hi> (S, A, Msb, K;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2839-2" target="ابتعثهُ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>. (TA, from a trad.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">بَعْثٌ</foreign> (S, K, TA) and <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثٌ</foreign> (TA) also signify The <hi rend="ital">quickening, vivifying,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">revivifying,</hi> of the dead; the <hi rend="ital">raising</hi> of the dead <hi rend="ital">to life;</hi> (S, K, * TA;) by God, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">on the day called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">يَوْمُ البَعْثِ</foreign> (S, TA) <hi rend="ital">the day</hi> [<hi rend="ital">of resurrection,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">when those who are in the graves shall be raised.</hi> (A, Mgh.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَ ٱللّٰهُ الخَلْقَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">المَوْتَى</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">God quickened, vivified, revivified,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">raised to life, mankind,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">the dead.</hi> (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">بَعِثَ</foreign>, aor.

[See <foreign lang="ar">بَعِثٌ</foreign>.]    </entryFree>26:Tf96,<entryFree id="n2841" key="انبعث" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>7</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">انبعث</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">أنبعث</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">انبعث</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ٱنبعث</orth>
                  </form> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He became sent;</hi> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">he went, being sent;</hi>] quasi-pass. of <foreign lang="ar">بَعَثَهُ</foreign>, as signifying “he sent him:” (S, Msb, K:) <hi rend="ital">he rose, and went away:</hi> (TA:) <hi rend="ital">he rose to go forth.</hi> (Bd in ix. 46.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">انبعث لِكَذَا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He went, being sent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he rose, and went away.</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he rose to go forth, for such a thing</hi> or <hi rend="ital">purpose</hi>]. (A, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">انبعث فُلَانٌ لِشَأْنِهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Such a one rose, and went away, to perform his affair.</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">انبعث فِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">السَّيْرِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He hastened, made haste, sped,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">was quick</hi> or <hi rend="ital">swift, in going, journeying,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">pace.</hi> (S.) And <foreign lang="ar">انبعث الشَّيْءُ</foreign>, i. e. <foreign lang="ar">اِنْدَفَعَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The thing became impelled,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">propelled;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">went quickly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">swiftly, as though impelled</hi> or <hi rend="ital">propelled;</hi> &amp;c.]; as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2841-1" target="تبعّث" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n2839"/></foreign>. (TA.) [Thus] you say, <foreign lang="ar">انبعث المَآءُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The water poured out,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">forth, as though impelled</hi> or <hi rend="ital">propelled</hi>]. (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">فجر</foreign>; &amp;c.) And [hence,] <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2841-2" target="تبعّث" n="2" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar" select="n2839"/>مِنِّىَ الشِّعْرُ</foreign>, i. e. <foreign lang="ar">انبعث</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The poetry issued quickly from me</hi>], as though it flowed (<foreign lang="ar">كَأَنَّهُ سَالَ</foreign>): so in the S and K: but in some of the copies of the S, in the place of <foreign lang="ar">سَالَ</foreign>, we find <foreign lang="ar">سَارَ</foreign>.
